<script>
var fpb_i=fpb_p=1;
var fpb_over=0;
var fpb_tID=null;
var fpb_timeout=5500;
fpb_tID=setTimeout(start_slideshow,fpb_timeout);

function start_slideshow()
  {
  if(fpb_tID) {clearTimeout(fpb_tID);fpb_tID=null;}
  if(!fpb_over)
    {
    show_fpbanner_item();
    fpb_tID = setTimeout(start_slideshow,fpb_timeout);
    }
  }
  
function show_fpbanner_item(n)
  {
  //console.log(n);
  fpb_p=fpb_i;
  if(isNaN(n)) n=++fpb_i;
  if(n>5) n=1;
  else if(n<1) n=5;
  
  fpb_i=n;
  if(fpb_over)
    {
    $('#images img, #info .title').hide();
    $('.btn_item').removeClass('active');
    $('#fb_i'+fpb_i).css('opacity',1).show();
    $('#fb_t'+fpb_i).css('opacity',1).show();
    $('#fb_b'+fpb_i).addClass('active');
    }
  else
    {
    $('#fb_i'+fpb_p).animate({opacity:0},1500,'linear',function(){
      $('#images img, #info .title').css('opacity',1).hide();
      $('#fb_i'+fpb_i).css('opacity',0).show().animate({opacity:1},1500);
      $('#fb_t'+fpb_i).css('opacity',1).show();
      $('.btn_item').removeClass('active');
      $('#fb_b'+fpb_i).addClass('active');
      });
    }
  }
$(function(){
  $('.btn_item').click(function(){
    show_fpbanner_item($(this).attr('rel'));
  });
  $('.fp_banner').mouseover(function(){fpb_over=1;});
  $('.fp_banner').mouseout(function(e){    
    var evt=e || window.event;
    var tgt = evt.relatedTarget || evt.toElement;
    var res=0;
    $.each($(tgt).parents(),function(k,v){if($('.fp_banner').get(0) == v) res=1;});
    if(!res)
      {
      fpb_over=0;
      fpb_tID=setTimeout(start_slideshow,fpb_timeout);
      }
    });
  $('#btn_left').click(function(){show_fpbanner_item(fpb_i-1);});


  $('#btn_right').click(function(){show_fpbanner_item(fpb_i+1);});
});
</script>

<script>
$(function(){
  $('.tab').click(function(){
    $('.tab').removeClass('selected');
    $(this).addClass('selected');
    var tab_id=$(this).attr('rel');
    
    $('#tab_'+tab_id).show();
    $('#tab_'+(tab_id==2?1:2)).hide();
    
  });
});
</script>

      $(function(){
        $('#addreview_city').focus(function(){
          $('#addreview_school_select').hide();
        });

        $('#addreview_school_input').focus(function(){
          $('#addreview_city_select').hide();
        });


        $('#addreview_city').bind('keypress keyup click',function(e){
            var city=$(this).val();
            var cities=city?str_in_array(city,all_cities):all_cities;

            e=e || window.event;
            var key=e.which || e.keyCode;
            if(key==13){
              var as=$(this).parent().find('.ajax_selector');
              as.children().first().click();
              $('.ajax_selector').hide();
              return false;
              };

            if(cities)
              {
              var html='';
              var cnt=cities.length;//items_num_in_ajax_select;
              $.each(cities,function(k,v){
                html+='<div rel="'+k+'">'+v+'</div>';
                if(--cnt<=0) return false;
              });
              if(html){$('#addreview_city_select').html(html).show();}
              else{$('#addreview_city_select').html('').hide();}
              }
            });

        $('#addreview_school_input').bind('keypress keyup click',function(e){


          e=e || window.event;
          var key=e.which || e.keyCode;
          if(key==13){
            var as=$(this).parent().find('.ajax_selector');
            as.children().first().click();
            $('.ajax_selector').hide();
            return false;
            };

          var school=$(this).val();
          var schools=school?str_in_array(school,all_city_shools):all_city_shools;

          if(schools)
            {
            var html='';
            var cnt=schools.length;//items_num_in_ajax_select;
            $.each(schools,function(k,v){
              html+='<div rel="'+k+'">'+v+'</div>';
              if(--cnt<=0) return false;
            });
            if(html){$('#addreview_school_select').html(html).show();}
            else{$('#addreview_school_select').html('').hide();$('#addreview_school').val('');}
            }
        });


        $(document).on(click_event,'#addreview_school_select div',function(){
          $('#'+$(this).parent().attr('rel')).val($(this).html().replace('&nbsp;',' '));
          $('#at_school_input').val($(this).html());
          $('#at_school').val($(this).attr('rel'));
          $('#addreview_school').val($(this).attr('rel'));
          //get_all_shool_teachers($(this).attr('rel'));
          $(this).parent().hide();
        });

        $(document).on(click_event,'#addreview_city_select div',function(){
          $('#'+$(this).parent().attr('rel')).val($(this).html());
          $('#as_city, #at_city').val($(this).html());
          $(this).parent().hide();
          $('#addreview_school, #addreview_school_input').val('');
          //reset_teacher_html();

          get_all_city_shools($(this).attr('rel'));
          //get_at_all_city_shools($(this).html());
        });
